### <a id="inductive-types-h-s-p-and-v">Inductive Types H, S, P, and V</a>

This section presents the [UALib.Varieties.Varieties][] module of the [Agda Universal Algebra Library][].

Fix a signature 𝑆, let 𝒦 be a class of 𝑆-algebras, and define

* H 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a homomorphic image of a members of 𝒦;
* S 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a subalgebra of a member of 𝒦;
* P 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a product of members of 𝒦.

A straight-forward verification confirms that H, S, and P are **closure operators** (expansive, monotone, and idempotent).  A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is said to be *closed under the taking of homomorphic images* provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. Similarly, 𝒦 is *closed under the taking of subalgebras* (resp., *arbitrary products*) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` (resp., `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`).

An algebra is a homomorphic image (resp., subalgebra; resp., product) of every algebra to which it is isomorphic. Thus, the class `H 𝒦` (resp., `S 𝒦`; resp., `P 𝒦`) is closed under isomorphism.

The operators H, S, and P can be composed with one another repeatedly, forming yet more closure operators.

<!-- If C₁ and C₂ are closure operators on classes of structures, let us say that C₁ ≤ C₂ if for every class 𝒦 we have C₁(𝒦) ⊆ C₂(𝒦). -->

A **variety** is a class 𝒦 of algebras in a fixed signature that is closed under the taking of homomorphic images (H), subalgebras (S), and arbitrary products (P).  That is, 𝒦 is a variety if and only if `H S P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`.

This module defines what we have found to be the most useful inductive types representing the closure operators H, S, and P. Separately, we define the inductive type `V` for simultaneously representing closure under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

<!-- ; consequently, we expect `V 𝒦 ≡ H (S (P 𝒦))` to hold for each class 𝒦 of algebras of a fixed signature. classes of algebras that are closed under H, S, P, and V ≡ HSP. -->

#### <a id="homomorphic-closure">Homomorphism closure</a>

We define the inductive type `H` to represent classes of algebras that include all homomorphic images of algebras in the class; i.e., classes that are closed under the taking of homomorphic images.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="2755" class="Comment">--Closure wrt H</a>

  <a id="H.hiso"></a><a id="3073" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3073" class="InductiveConstructor">hiso</a>  <a id="3079" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3081" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3082" <!-- We say that a class 𝒦 is **closed under** `H` (or `H`-**closed**) provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. -->

--------------------------------

#### <a id="subalgebra-closure">Subalgebra closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing classes of algebras that are closed under the taking of subalgebras as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3521" class="Comment">--Closure wrt S</a>
<a id="3537" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="S"></a><a id="3542" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3542" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="3544" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3545" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3545" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3547" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3547" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="3549" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3551" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="3559" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="3561" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3561" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3563" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3565" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3570" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3571" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3579" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3545" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3581" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3582" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3584" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3585" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="3588" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3545" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="3589" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3592" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="3595" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3600" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3601" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3609" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3610" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3545" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3612" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3614" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3547" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3615" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3617" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3618" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3620" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3621" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="3624" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3625" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3545" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3627" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3629" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3547" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3630" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3633" class="Keyword">where</a>

href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3561" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

<!-- A class 𝒦 is **closed under** `S` (or `S`-**closed**) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` -->

-----------------------------------------

#### <a id="product-closure">Product closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing classes of algebras closed under arbitrary products is the following. 

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="4325" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="P"></a><a id="4330" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4332" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4333" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4335" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4335" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="4337" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4339" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="4347" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4349" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4350" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4350" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4352" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4354" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="4359" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4360" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4368" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4370" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4371" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4373" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4374" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="4377" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4378" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4381" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="4384" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="4389" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4390" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4398" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4399" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4401" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4403" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4335" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4404" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4406" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4407" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4409" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4410" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="4413" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4414" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4416" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4418" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4335" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4419" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4422" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="P.pbase"></a><a id="4430" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4430" class="InductiveConstructor">pbase</a>  <a id="4437" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4439" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4440" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4440" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4442" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4444" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4452" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4333" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4454" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4455" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4457" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4459" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4440" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4461" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4463" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4350" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4465" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4467" href="UALib.Algebras.Lifts.html#3828" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="4476" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4440" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4478" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4335" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="4480" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4482" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4484" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4350" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

  <a id="P.prodw"></a><a id="4715" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4715" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a>  <a id="4722" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4724" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4725" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4779" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4781" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4350" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="4782" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4784" class="Symbol">→</a> <a class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4864" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4825" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4866" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4868" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4825" </pre>

<!-- A class 𝒦 is **closed under** `P` (or `P`-**closed**) provided `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. -->

-----------------------------------------------

#### <a id="variety-closure">Varietal closure</a>

A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is called a **variety** if it is closed under each of the closure operators H, S, and P introduced above; the corresponding closure operator is often denoted 𝕍, but we will typically denote it by `V`.

Thus, if 𝒦 is a class of 𝑆-algebras, then the **variety generated by** 𝒦 is denoted by `V 𝒦` and defined to be the smallest class that contains 𝒦 and is closed under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

We now define `V` as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="5605" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="V"></a><a id="5610" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5610" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5612" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5613" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5613" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5615" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5615" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="5617" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5619" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="5627" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="5629" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5629" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5631" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5633" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5638" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5639" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5647" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5613" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5649" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5650" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5652" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5653" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="5656" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5613" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5657" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5660" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="5663" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5668" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5669" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5677" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5678" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5613" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5680" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5682" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5615" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5683" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5685" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5686" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5688" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="5691" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5692" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5613" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5694" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5696" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5615" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5697" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5700" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="V.vbase"></a><a id="5708" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5708" class="InductiveConstructor">vbase</a>  <a id="5715" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5717" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5718" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5718" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5720" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5722" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5730" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5613" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5732" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5733" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5735" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5737" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5718" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5739" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5741" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5629" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5743" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5745" href="UALib.Algebras.Lifts.html#3828" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="5754" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5718" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5756" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5615" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="5758" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5760" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5610" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5762" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5629" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

-------------------------------

#### <a id="closure-properties">Closure properties</a>

The types defined above represent operators with useful closure properties. We now prove a handful of such properties since we will need them later.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="6701" class="Comment">-- P is a closure operator, in particular, it&#39;s expansive...</a>
<a id="P-expa"></a><a id="6762" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6762" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="6769" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6771" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6772" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6772" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6774" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6776" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="6784" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6786" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6786" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6788" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6790" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="6795" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6796" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6804" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6772" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6806" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6807" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="6809" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="6812" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6772" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6813" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="6817" class="Symbol">→</a>       <a id="6825" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6786" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6827" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2949" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="6829" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="6830" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6831" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6772" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6832" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6834" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6772" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6835" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6837" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6786" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

We sometimes want to go back and forth between our two representations of subalgebras of algebras in a class. The tools `subalgebra→S` and `S→subalgebra` are made for that purpose.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="subalgebra→S"></a><a id="8639" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8639" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="8652" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8654" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8655" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8655" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8657" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8657" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="8659" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8661" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="8669" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8671" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8671" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="8673" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8675" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="8680" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8681" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8689" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8655" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8691" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8692" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="8694" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="8697" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8655" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="8698" class="Symbol">)}</a>
               <a id="8716" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8717" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8717" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8719" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8721" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8729" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8730" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8655" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8732" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="8734" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8657" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="8735" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8737" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8738" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8740" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8742" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8717" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8744" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2536" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="8764" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8671" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

Next we observe that lifting to a higher universe does not break the property of being a subalgebra of an algebra of a class.  In other words, if we lift a subalgebra of an algebra in a class, the result is still a subalgebra of an algebra in the class.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="lift-alg-subP"></a><a id="10928" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10928" class="Function">lift-alg-subP</a> <a id="10942" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10944" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10945" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10945" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10947" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10947" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="10949" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10951" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="10959" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10961" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10961" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="10963" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10965" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="10970" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10971" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10979" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10945" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10981" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10982" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="10984" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="10987" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10945" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10988" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="10991" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10991" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10993" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10995" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="11003" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10945" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="11005" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="11006" class="Symbol">}</a>

 <a id="11010" class="Symbol">→</a>                <a id="11027" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10991" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="11029" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2536" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="11049" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11050" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="11051" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11052" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10945" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="11053" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="11055" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10945" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="11056" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11058" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10961" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="11059" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="11408" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11408" class="Function">plA</a> <a id="11412" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11414" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11257" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="11417" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="11419" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="11420" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11421" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11201" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="11422" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="11424" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11205" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="11425" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11427" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11209" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="11431" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11408" class="Function">plA</a> <a id="11435" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11437" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4488" class="InductiveConstructor">pliftu</a> <a id="11444" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11233" class="Bound">pA</a>

  <a id="11450" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11450" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="11452" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11454" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11260" class="Function">lB</a> <a id="11457" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2536" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="11477" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11478" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="11479" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11480" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11201" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="11481" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="11483" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11205" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="11484" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11486" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11209" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="11487" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="11491" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11450" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="11493" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11495" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11257" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="11498" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#5763" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="11500" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11501" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11263" class="Function">lC</a> <a id="11504" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#5763" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="11506" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11349" class="Function">lC≤lA</a><a id="11511" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11513" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#5763" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="11515" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11408" class="Function">plA</a> <a id="11519" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#5763" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="11521" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11522" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5261" class="Function">lift-alg-iso</a> <a id="11535" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11201" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="11537" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11205" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="11539" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11213" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="11541" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11222" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="11543" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11238" class="Bound">B≅C</a><a id="11546" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

The next lemma would be too obvoius to care about were it not for the fact that we'll need it later, so it too must be formalized.

We need to formalize one more lemma before arriving the short term objective of this section, which is the proof of the inclusion PS⊆SP.

<pre class="Agda">

  <a id="14821" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14821" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="14823" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14825" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14827" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13986" class="Bound">ℬ</a> <a id="14829" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="14831" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="14833" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14130" class="Function">SA</a>
  <a id="14838" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14821" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="14840" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14842" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6161" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="14845" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2277" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="14849" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14238" class="Function">B≅SA</a>

</pre>

#### PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦)

Finally, we are in a position to prove that a product of subalgebras of algebras in a class 𝒦 is a subalgebra of a product of algebras in 𝒦.

<pre class="Agda">

   <a id="17470" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17470" class="Function">spA</a> <a id="17474" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17476" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17406" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="17478" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="17480" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3542" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="17481" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17482" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15135" class="Function">𝓾</a><a id="17483" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17485" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15135" class="Function">𝓾</a><a id="17486" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17488" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17489" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="17490" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17491" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15053" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17492" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17494" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15135" class="Function">𝓾</a><a id="17495" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17497" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15067" class="Bound">𝒦u</a><a id="17499" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="17504" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17470" class="Function">spA</a> <a id="17508" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17510" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15160" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="17516" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17412" class="Bound">pA</a>

</pre>

#### <a id="more-class-inclusions">More class inclusions</a>

We conclude this module with three more inclusion relations that will have bit parts to play in our formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem.

 <a id="18387" class="Symbol">→</a>    <a id="18392" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3542" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="18393" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18394" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18340" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18396" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="18398" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18342" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="18399" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18401" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18340" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18403" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="18405" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18342" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="18406" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18408" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18409" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="18410" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18411" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18340" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18412" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18414" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18342" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="18415" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18417" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18356" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18418" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18420" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2949" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="18422" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5610" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="18423" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18424" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18340" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18425" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18427" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18342" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="18428" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18430" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18356" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
<a id="18432" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18332" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18437" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18438" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3641" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a><a id="18443" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18444" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18444" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18445" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18447" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18447" class="Bound">PCloA</a><a id="18452" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18454" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18456" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17745" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="18460" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18461" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4878" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="18467" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18447" class="Bound">PCloA</a> <a id="18473" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4327" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="18483" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="18485" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18332" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18490" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18491" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3698" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a><a id="18496" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18497" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18497" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18498" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18500" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18500" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18501" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18503" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18505" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5832" class="InductiveConstructor">vliftw</a> <a id="18512" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18513" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18332" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18518" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18500" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18519" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="18521" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18332" class="Function">SP⊆V</a><a id="18525" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18526" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18526" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18527" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18529" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18529" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="18530" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18532" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18533" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18533" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18534" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18536" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18537" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3763" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a><a id="18541" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18542" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18542" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18543" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18545" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18545" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="18546" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18548" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18548" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="18552" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18552" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="18555" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18557" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18559" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6063" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="18566" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18567" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18332" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18572" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18548" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="18575" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18577" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18552" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="18581" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18332" class="Function">SP⊆V</a><a id="18585" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18586" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18586" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18587" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18589" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18589" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="18590" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18592" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18593" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18593" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18594" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18596" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18597" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3842" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a><a id="18602" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18603" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18603" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18604" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18606" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18606" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="18607" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18609" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18609" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="18613" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18613" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="18616" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18618" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18620" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6063" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="18627" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18628" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18332" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18633" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18609" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="18636" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18638" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18613" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="18642" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18332" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18647" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18648" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3906" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="18653" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18653" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="18655" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18655" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="18657" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18659" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18661" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6372" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="18667" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18668" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18332" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="18673" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18653" class="Bound">x</a><a id="18674" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18676" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18655" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="products-of-classes">Products of classes</a>

Above we proved PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦).  It is slightly more painful to prove that the product of *all* algebras in the class S(𝒦) is a member of SP(𝒦). That is,

```agda
⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)
```

This is mainly due to the fact that it's not obvious (at least not to this author-coder) what should be the type of the product of all members of a class of algebras.  After a few false starts, eventually the right type revealed itself.  Of course, now that we have it in our hands, it seems rather obvious.

We now describe the this type of product of all algebras in an arbitrary class 𝒦 of algebras of the same signature.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="19373" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="class-product"></a><a id="19380" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19380" class="Module">class-product</a> <a id="19394" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19395" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19395" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19397" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19399" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="19407" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19409" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19409" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19411" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19413" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="19418" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19419" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19427" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19395" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19429" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19430" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19432" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19433" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="19436" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19395" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19437" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="19440" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="19448" class="Comment">-- ℑ serves as the index of the product</a>
 <a id="class-product.ℑ"></a><a id="19489" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19489" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="19491" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19493" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19494" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19494" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19496" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19498" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="19506" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19508" class="Symbol">→</a>  <a id="19511" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="19516" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19517" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19525" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19494" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19527" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19528" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19530" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="19533" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19494" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19534" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19536" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19538" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19539" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="19542" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19494" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19543" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19545" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
 <a id="19548" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19489" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="19550" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19551" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19551" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19552" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19554" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19554" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19556" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19558" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="19560" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="19562" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="19564" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19565" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19573" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19551" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19575" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19576" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19578" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="19580" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19560" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="19582" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19584" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19554" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

  <a id="19589" class="Comment">-- 𝔄 produces an algebra for each index (i : ℑ).</a>
 <a id="class-product.𝔄"></a><a id="19639" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19639" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="19641" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19643" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19644" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19644" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19646" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19648" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="19656" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19658" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19658" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19660" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19662" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="19667" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19668" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19676" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19644" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19678" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19679" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19681" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="19684" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19644" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19685" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="19688" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19690" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19489" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="19692" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19658" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19694" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19696" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19704" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19644" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19706" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="19709" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19639" class="Function">𝔄</a><a id="19710" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19711" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19711" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19712" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19714" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19714" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19715" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19717" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19719" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="19721" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19722" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19722" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19724" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19726" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19727" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19489" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="19729" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19714" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19730" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19733" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19735" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="19737" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19722" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19739" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

 <a id="19743" class="Comment">-- The product of all members of 𝒦 can be written simply as follows:</a>
 <a id="class-product.class-product"></a><a id="19813" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19813" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="19827" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19829" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19830" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19830" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19832" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19834" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="19842" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19844" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19846" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="19851" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19852" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19860" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19830" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19862" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19863" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19865" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="19868" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19830" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19869" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19871" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19873" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19881" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19882" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="19885" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19830" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19886" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19888" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="19891" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19813" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="19905" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19906" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19906" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19907" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19909" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19909" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19911" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19913" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="19915" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19917" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19639" class="Function">𝔄</a><a id="19918" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19919" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19906" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19920" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19922" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19909" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19923" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19925" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="19929" class="Comment">-- ...or, more explicitly, here is the expansion of this indexed product.</a>
 <a id="class-product.class-product&#39;"></a><a id="20004" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20004" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a> <a id="20019" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20021" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20022" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20022" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="20024" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20026" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="20034" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20036" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20038" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="20043" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20044" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="20052" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20022" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="20054" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="20055" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="20057" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="20060" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20022" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="20061" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20063" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20065" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="20073" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20074" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="20077" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20022" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="20078" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20080" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="20083" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20004" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a><a id="20097" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20098" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20098" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="20099" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20101" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20101" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="20103" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20105" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="20107" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="20109" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20110" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20110" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="20112" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20114" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20115" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="20117" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20117" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="20119" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="20121" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20122" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="20130" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20098" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="20132" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="20133" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20135" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="20137" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20117" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="20139" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="20141" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20101" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="20142" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="20145" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20147" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="20149" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20110" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="20151" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

</pre>

Notice that, if `p : 𝑨 ∈ 𝒦`, then we can think of the pair `(𝑨 , p) ∈ ℑ 𝒦` as an index over the class, and so we can think of `𝔄 (𝑨 , p)` (which is obviously `𝑨`) as the projection of the product `⨅ ( 𝔄{𝓤}{𝒦} )` onto the `(𝑨 , p)`-th component.

#### ⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)
Finally, we prove the result that plays a leading role in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem---namely, that our newly defined class product ⨅ ( 𝔄{𝓤}{𝒦} ) belongs to SP(𝒦).

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="20623" class="Comment">-- The product of all subalgebras of a class 𝒦 belongs to SP(𝒦).</a>
<a id="20688" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="class-product-inclusions"></a><a id="20695" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20695" class="Module">class-product-inclusions</a> <a id="20720" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20721" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20721" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="20723" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20725" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="20733" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20735" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20736" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20736" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="20738" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20740" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1066" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="20745" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20746" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#811" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="20754" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20721" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="20756" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2258" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="20757" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="20759" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="20762" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20721" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="20763" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="20766" class="Keyword">where</a>

   <a id="21567" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#21567" class="Function">⨅llA≅cpK</a> <a id="21576" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21578" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#678" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="21580" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#21064" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="21584" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="21586" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19813" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="21600" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21601" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3542" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="21602" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21603" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20721" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21604" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="21606" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20721" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21607" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21609" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20736" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="21610" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="21615" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#21567" class="Function">⨅llA≅cpK</a> <a id="21624" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21626" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6161" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="21629" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2277" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="21633" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#21456" class="Function">llA≅A</a>

 <a id="21641" class="Comment">-- So, since PS⊆SP, we see that that the product of all subalgebras of a class 𝒦 belongs to SP(𝒦).</a>

  <a id="21785" class="Symbol">→</a>                  <a id="21804" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19813" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="21818" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21819" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3542" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="21820" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21821" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20721" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21822" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="21824" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20721" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21825" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21827" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20736" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="21828" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21830" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2667" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="21832" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21833" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3542" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="21834" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21835" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="21838" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20721" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21839" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="21841" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="21844" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20721" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21845" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21847" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21848" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="21849" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21850" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20721" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21851" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="21853" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2273" class="Function">OV</a> <a id="21856" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20721" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="21857" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21859" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20736" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="21860" class="Symbol">))</a>
